3922       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3923       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, Type::Offset(0));
3924       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3925       cast->init_req(0, control());
3926       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3927     }
3928 
3929     Node* original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3930     // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3931     // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3932     // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3933     // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3934     // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3935     // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3936     // the input array from type speculation.
3937     if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton() && !stopped()) {
3938       ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(original_kls)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3939       ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3940 
3941       int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3942       if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3943         const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3944         if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3945           original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3946           original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3947         }
3948       }
3949     }
3950 
3951     if (UseFlatArray) {
3952       // Either both or neither new array klass and original array
3953       // klass must be flattened
3954       const TypeAryPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->isa_aryptr();
3955       Node* is_flat = generate_flatArray_guard(klass_node, NULL);
3956       if (t_original == NULL || !t_original->is_not_flat()) {
3957         generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, bailout);
3958       }
3959       if (is_flat != NULL) {
3960         RegionNode* r = new RegionNode(2);
3961         record_for_igvn(r);
3962         r->init_req(1, control());
3963         set_control(is_flat);
3964         if (t_original == NULL || !t_original->is_not_flat()) {
3965           generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, r);
3966         }
3967         bailout->add_req(control());
3968         set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
3969       }
3970     }
3971 
3972     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
3973     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
3974     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
3975 
3976     Node* length = end;
3977     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
3978       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
3979     }
3980 
3981     // Bail out if length is negative.
3982     // Without this the new_array would throw
3983     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
3984     // should be thrown
3985     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
3986 
3987     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
3988       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3989       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
3990       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
3991                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
3992     }
3993 
3994     if (!stopped()) {
3995       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
3996       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
3997       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
3998       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
3999 
4000       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4001       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
4002       // oop stores need checking.
4003       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
4004       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
4005 
4006       bool validated = false;
4007       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
4008       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
4009       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
4010         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(original, klass_node);
4011 
4012         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4013           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4014           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4015           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
4016                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4017           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4018         }
4019         validated = true;
4020       }
4021 
4022       if (!stopped()) {
4023         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0);  // no arguments to push
4024 
4025         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
4026                                                 original_kls, klass_node);
4027         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
4028           ac->set_copyof(validated);
4029         } else {
4030           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
4031         }
4032         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4033         if (n == ac) {
4034           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4035         } else {
4036           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4037           set_all_memory(n);
4038         }
4039       }
4040     }
4041   } // original reexecute is set back here
4042 
4043   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4044   if (!stopped()) {
4045     set_result(newcopy);
4046   }
4047   return true;
4048 }
4049 
4050 
4051 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
4052 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
4053 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
4054                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
4055   ciMethod* method = callee();
4056   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4057   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4058          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4059   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
4060   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
4061                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
4062                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
4063   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
4064   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
4065 
4066   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
4067   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
4068 
4069   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
4070   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
4071   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
4072 
4073   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
4074 }
4075 
4076 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
4077 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
4078 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
4079 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
4080 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
4081 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
4082 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
4083 CallJavaNode*
4084 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4085   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
4086   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
4087 
4088   ciMethod* method = callee();
4089   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
4090   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
4091 
4092   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
4093   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
4094   if (is_static) {
4095     assert(!is_virtual, "");
4096     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4097                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
4098                            method, bci());
4099   } else if (is_virtual) {
4100     null_check_receiver();
4101     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
4102     if (UseInlineCaches) {
4103       // Suppress the vtable call
4104     } else {
4105       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
4106       // so the vtable index is fixed.
4107       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
4108        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4109        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4110               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4111     }
4112     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
4113                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
4114                           method, vtable_index, bci());
4115   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
4116     null_check_receiver();
4117     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4118                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
4119                                 method, bci());
4120     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
4121   }
4122   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
4123     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
4124     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
4125     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
4126     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
4127     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
4128   }
4129   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
4130   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
4131   return slow_call;
4132 }
4133 
4134 
4135 /**
4136  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
4137  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
4138  * slightly different code.
4139  */
4140 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4141   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
4142   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
4143 
4144   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
4145 
4146   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4147   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
4148   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4149   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4150   Node* obj = argument(0);
4151 
4152   if (obj->is_InlineType() || gvn().type(obj)->is_inlinetypeptr()) {
4153     return false;
4154   }
4155 
4156   if (!is_static) {
4157     // Check for hashing null object
4158     obj = null_check_receiver();
4159     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
4160     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
4161     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
4162   } else {
4163     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
4164     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
4165     Node* null_ctl = top();
4166     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
4167     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
4168     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
4169   }
4170 
4171   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
4172   if (stopped()) {
4173     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
4174     if (!stopped())
4175       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
4176     return true;
4177   }
4178 
4179   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
4180   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4181   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4182   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4183 
4184   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
4185   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
4186   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
4187   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4188   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
4189   // Object hashCode().
4190   if (is_virtual) {
4191     // After null check, get the object's klass.
4192     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4193     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4194   }
4195 
4196   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
4197   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
4198   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
4199   // the null check after castPP removal.
4200   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
4201   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
4202 
4203   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
4204   // This also serves as guard against inline types (they have the always_locked_pattern set).
4205   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
4206   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
4207   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
4208   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
4209   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
4210 
4211   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
4212 
4213   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
4214   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
4215   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
4216   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
4217   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
4218   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
4219   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
4220   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
4221   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
4222   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
4223   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
4224   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
4225   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
4226 
4227   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
4228   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
4229   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
4230 
4231   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
4232 
4233   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
4234   // fill in the rest of the null path:
4235   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
4236   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
4237 
4238   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
4239   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
4240   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
4241   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
4242 
4243   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
4244   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4245   if (!stopped()) {
4246     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
4247     set_all_memory(init_mem);
4248     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
4249     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
4250     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
4251     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4252     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4253     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4254     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4255     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4256   }
4257 
4258   // Return the combined state.
4259   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
4260   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4261 
4262   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
4263   return true;
4264 }
4265 
4266 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
4267 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
4268 //
4269 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
4270 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
4271   Node* obj = argument(0);
4272   if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4273     ciKlass* vk = _gvn.type(obj)->inline_klass();
4274     set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(vk->java_mirror())));
4275     return true;
4276   }
4277   obj = null_check_receiver();
4278   if (stopped())  return true;
4279   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
4280   return true;
4281 }
4282 
4283 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
4284 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
4285 //
4286 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
4287 //
4288 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
4289 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
4290 // caller sensitive methods.
4291 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
4292 #ifndef PRODUCT
4293   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4294     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
4295   }
4296 #endif
4297 
4298   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
4299 #ifndef PRODUCT
4300     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4301       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
4302     }
4303 #endif
4304     return false;
4305   }
4306 
4307   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
4308   // depth.
4309   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
4310 
4311   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
4312   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
4313   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
4314   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
4315     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
4316     switch (n) {
4317     case 0:
4318       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
4319       break;
4320     case 1:
4321       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
4322       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
4323 #ifndef PRODUCT
4324         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4325           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4326         }
4327 #endif
4328         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4329       }
4330       break;
4331     default:
4332       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4333         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4334         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4335         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4336         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4337         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4338 
4339 #ifndef PRODUCT
4340         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4341           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4342           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4343           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4344             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4345             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4346           }
4347         }
4348 #endif
4349         return true;
4350       }
4351       break;
4352     }
4353   }
4354 
4355 #ifndef PRODUCT
4356   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4357     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4358     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4359     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4360       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4361       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4362     }
4363   }
4364 #endif
4365 
4366   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4367 }
4368 
4369 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4370   Node* arg = argument(0);
4371   Node* result = NULL;
4372 
4373   switch (id) {
4374   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4375   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4376   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4377   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4378 
4379   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4380     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4381     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4382     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4383 
4384     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4385     // Build the boolean node
4386     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4387 
4388     // Branch either way.
4389     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4390     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4391     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4392     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4393     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4394     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4395 
4396     set_control(iftrue);
4397 
4398     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4399     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4400     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4401     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4402 
4403     // Else fall through
4404     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4405     set_control(iffalse);
4406 
4407     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4408     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4409 
4410     // Post merge
4411     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4412     record_for_igvn(r);
4413 
4414     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4415     result = phi;
4416     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4417     break;
4418   }
4419 
4420   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4421     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4422     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4423     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4424 
4425     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4426     // Build the boolean node
4427     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4428 
4429     // Branch either way.
4430     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4431     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4432     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4433     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4434     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4435     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4436 
4437     set_control(iftrue);
4438 
4439     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4440     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4441     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4442     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4443 
4444     // Else fall through
4445     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4446     set_control(iffalse);
4447 
4448     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4449     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4450 
4451     // Post merge
4452     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4453     record_for_igvn(r);
4454 
4455     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4456     result = phi;
4457     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4458     break;
4459   }
4460 
4461   default:
4462     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4463     break;
4464   }
4465   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4466   return true;
4467 }
4468 
4469 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4470 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4471 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4472   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4473   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4474   if (stopped())  return true;
4475 
4476   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4477 
4478   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4479   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4480   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4481   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4482   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4483 
4484   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4485          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4486 
4487   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4488   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4489 
4490   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4491   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4492   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4493 
4494   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4495   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4496   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4497   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4498 
4499   // update volatile field
4500   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4501 
4502   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4503   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4504                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4505                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4506                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4507                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4508                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4509 
4510   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4511 
4512   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4513   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4514 
4515   return true;
4516 }
4517 
4518 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4519 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4520 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4521   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4522   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4523   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4524 
4525   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4526   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4527     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4528     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4529     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4530     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4531     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4532     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4533     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4534     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4535     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4536   }
4537 
4538   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4539   // Exclude the header but include array length to copy by 8 bytes words.
4540   // Can't use base_offset_in_bytes(bt) since basic type is unknown.
4541   int base_off = BarrierSetC2::arraycopy_payload_base_offset(is_array);
4542   Node* countx = size;
4543   countx = _gvn.transform(new SubXNode(countx, MakeConX(base_off)));
4544   countx = _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(countx, intcon(LogBytesPerLong)));
4545 
4546   access_clone(obj, alloc_obj, countx, is_array);
4547 
4548   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4549   if (alloc != NULL) {
4550     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4551     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4552     // other threads.
4553     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4554     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4555     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4556     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4557     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4558   } else {
4559     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4560   }
4561 }
4562 
4563 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4564 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4565 //
4566 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4567 //  null receiver => normal trap
4568 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4569 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4570 //
4571 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4572 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4573 //
4574 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4575 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4576 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4577 //
4578 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4579 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4580 //
4581 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4582   PhiNode* result_val;
4583 
4584   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4585   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4586   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4587     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4588 
4589     Node* obj = argument(0);
4590     if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4591       return false;
4592     }
4593 
4594     obj = null_check_receiver();
4595     if (stopped())  return true;
4596 
4597     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4598 
4599     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4600     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4601     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4602     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4603         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4604         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass() &&
4605         !obj_type->speculative_type()->is_inlinetype()) {
4606       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4607       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4608           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4609         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4610         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4611             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4612             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4613           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4614         }
4615       }
4616     }
4617 
4618     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4619     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4620     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4621 
4622     // paths into result_reg:
4623     enum {
4624       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4625       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4626       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4627       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4628       PATH_LIMIT
4629     };
4630     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4631     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4632     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4633     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4634     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4635 
4636     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4637     // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4638     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4639     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4640     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4641 
4642     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4643     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4644       // It's an array.
4645       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4646       set_control(array_ctl);
4647 
4648       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4649       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) &&
4650           UseFlatArray && obj_type->klass()->can_be_inline_array_klass() &&
4651           (!obj_type->isa_aryptr() || !obj_type->is_aryptr()->is_not_flat())) {
4652         // Flattened inline type array may have object field that would require a
4653         // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
4654         generate_flatArray_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4655       }
4656 
4657       if (!stopped()) {
4658         Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4659         Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4660         Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4661 
4662         BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4663         if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4664           // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4665           // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4666           Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4667           if (is_obja != NULL) {
4668             PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4669             set_control(is_obja);
4670             // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4671             Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4672             ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4673             ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4674             Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4675             assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4676             ac->connect_outputs(this, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4677 
4678             result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4679             result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4680             result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4681             result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4682           }
4683         }
4684         // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4685         // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4686         //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4687         //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4688         //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4689         //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4690         //  the object.)
4691 
4692         if (!stopped()) {
4693           copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4694 
4695           // Present the results of the copy.
4696           result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4697           result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4698           result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4699           result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4700         }
4701       }
4702     }
4703 
4704     if (!stopped()) {
4705       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4706       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4707       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4708       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4709       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4710       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4711       // Object clone().
4712       if (is_virtual) {
4713         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4714       }
4715 
4716       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4717       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4718       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4719       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4720                                   // Test both conditions:
4721                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4722                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4723                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4724                                   slow_region);
4725     }
4726 
4727     if (!stopped()) {
4728       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4729       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4730       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4731       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4732       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4733       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4734       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4735 
4736       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4737 
4738       // Present the results of the slow call.
4739       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4740       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4741       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4742       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4743     }
4744 
4745     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4746     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4747     if (!stopped()) {
4748       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4749       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4750       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4751       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4752       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4753       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4754       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4755       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4756       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4757     }
4758 
4759     // Return the combined state.
4760     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4761     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4762     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4763   } // original reexecute is set back here
4764 
4765   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4766   return true;
4767 }
4768 
4769 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4770 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4771 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4772 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4773 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4774 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4775 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4776 // initialization.
4777 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4778   if (alloc != NULL) {
4779     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4780     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4781 
4782     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4783         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4784       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4785       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4786       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4787       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4788       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4789       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4790         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4791           Node* n = mms.memory();
4792           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4793             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4794             no_interfering_store = false;
4795             break;
4796           }
4797         }
4798       } else {
4799         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4800           Node* n = mms.memory();
4801           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4802             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4803             no_interfering_store = false;
4804             break;
4805           }
4806         }
4807       }
4808 
4809       if (no_interfering_store) {
4810         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4811         uint size = alloc->req();
4812         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4813         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4814         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4815           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4816         }
4817         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4818         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4819         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4820         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4821         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4822         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4823         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4824 
4825         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4826         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4827         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4828 
4829         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4830         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4831 
4832         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4833         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4834 
4835         return saved_jvms;
4836       }
4837     }
4838   }
4839   return NULL;
4840 }
4841 
4842 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4843 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4844 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4845 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4846 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4847 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4848 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4849 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4850                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4851   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4852     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4853     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4854     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4855     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4856     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4857     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4858     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4859     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4860     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4861     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4862 
4863     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4864     CallProjections* callprojs = alloc->extract_projections(true);
4865     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4866     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4867     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4868     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4869     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4870 
4871     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4872     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4873     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4874     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4875     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4876     set_all_memory(mem);
4877     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4878     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4879     set_i_o(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj);
4880 
4881     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4882     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4883     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4884     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4885       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4886     }
4887     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4888     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4889     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4890     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4891 
4892     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4893     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4894     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4895 
4896     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4897     dest->set_req(0, control());
4898     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4899     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4900   }
4901 }
4902 
4903 
4904 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4905 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4906 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4907 //                                                      int length);
4908 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4909   // Get the arguments.
4910   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4911   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4912   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4913   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4914   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4915 
4916   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4917 
4918   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4919   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4920   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4921 
4922   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4923   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4924   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4925   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4926   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4927   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4928   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4929 
4930   // The following tests must be performed
4931   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4932   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4933   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4934   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4935   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4936   // (6) length must not be negative.
4937   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4938   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4939   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4940 
4941   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4942   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4943   Node* null_ctl = top();
4944   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4945   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4946   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4947 
4948   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4949     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4950     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4951     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4952     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4953     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4954     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4955     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4956     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4957   }
4958 
4959   bool validated = false;
4960 
4961   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4962   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
4963   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4964   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4965 
4966   // Do we have the type of src?
4967   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4968   // Do we have the type of dest?
4969   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4970   // Is the type for src from speculation?
4971   bool src_spec = false;
4972   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
4973   bool dest_spec = false;
4974 
4975   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
4976     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
4977     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
4978     // and dest so that it pays off.
4979 
4980     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
4981     bool could_have_src = has_src;
4982     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
4983     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
4984 
4985     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
4986     if (!has_src) {
4987       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4988       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
4989         could_have_src = true;
4990       }
4991     }
4992 
4993     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
4994     if (!has_dest) {
4995       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4996       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
4997         could_have_dest = true;
4998       }
4999     }
5000 
5001     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5002       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5003       if (!has_src) {
5004         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5005         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5006         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5007         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5008         src_spec = true;
5009       }
5010       if (!has_dest) {
5011         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5012         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5013         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5014         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5015         dest_spec = true;
5016       }
5017     }
5018   }
5019 
5020   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5021     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5022     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5023     if (is_reference_type(src_elem))   src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5024     if (is_reference_type(dest_elem))  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5025 
5026     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5027       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5028       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5029       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5030       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5031       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5032       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5033       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5034       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5035       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5036       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5037       if (!src_spec) {
5038         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5039         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5040           could_have_src = true;
5041         }
5042       }
5043       if (!dest_spec) {
5044         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5045         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5046           could_have_dest = true;
5047         }
5048       }
5049       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5050         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5051         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5052           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5053           src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5054           top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5055         }
5056         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5057           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5058           dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
5059           top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5060         }
5061       }
5062     }
5063   }
5064 
5065   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5066   int trap_bci = bci();
5067   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5068     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5069     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5070   }
5071 
5072   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5073 
5074   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5075       can_emit_guards &&
5076       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5077     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5078     validated = true;
5079 
5080     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5081     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5082 
5083     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5084     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5085     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5086 
5087     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5088     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5089 
5090     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5091     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5092 
5093     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5094     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5095 
5096     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5097     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5098                          load_array_length(src),
5099                          slow_region);
5100 
5101     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5102     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5103                          load_array_length(dest),
5104                          slow_region);
5105 
5106     // (6) length must not be negative.
5107     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5108     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5109     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5110     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5111       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5112       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5113     }
5114 
5115     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5116     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5117     if (src != dest) {
5118       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5119 
5120       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5121         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5122         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5123         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5124                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5125         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5126       }
5127     }
5128 
5129     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5130     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5131     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5132     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5133     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5134 
5135     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->is_flat() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5136       generate_flatArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5137       top_dest = top_dest->cast_to_not_flat();
5138       dest = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), dest, top_dest));
5139     }
5140     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->is_flat() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5141       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5142       generate_flatArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5143       top_src = top_src->cast_to_not_flat();
5144       src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, top_src));
5145     }
5146 
5147     {
5148       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5149       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5150       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5151                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5152       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5153     }
5154   }
5155 
5156   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5157 
5158   if (stopped()) {
5159     return true;
5160   }
5161 
5162   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5163                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5164                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5165                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5166                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5167                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5168 
5169   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5170 
5171   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5172   if (n == ac) {
5173     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5174   } else {
5175     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5176     set_all_memory(n);
5177   }
5178   clear_upper_avx();
5179 
5180 
5181   return true;
5182 }
5183 
5184 
5185 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5186 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5187 AllocateArrayNode*
5188 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5189                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5190   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5191   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5192 
5193   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5194   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5195 
5196   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5197   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5198   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5199     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5200     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5201     return NULL;
5202   }
5203   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5204   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5205     return NULL;
5206   }
5207 
5208   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5209   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5210     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5211     if (obs != this->map()) {
5212       return NULL;
5213     }
5214   }
5215 
5216   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5217   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5218   Node* ctl = control();
5219   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5220     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5221     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5222     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5223     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5224       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5225       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5226       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5227       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5228         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5229         continue;
5230       }
5231       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5232       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5233       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5234       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5235       bool found_trap = false;
5236       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5237         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5238         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5239             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5240           found_trap = true; break;
5241         }
5242       }
5243       if (found_trap) {
5244         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5245         continue;
5246       }
5247     }
5248     return NULL;
5249   }
5250 
5251   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5252   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5253   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5254   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5255 
5256   return alloc;
5257 }
5258 
5259 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5260 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5261 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5262   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5263   // no receiver since it is static method
5264   Node *src         = argument(0);
5265   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5266   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5267   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5268   Node *length      = argument(4);
5269 
5270   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5271   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5272 
5273   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5274   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5275   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5276   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5277   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5278       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5279     // failed array check
5280     return false;
5281   }
5282 
5283   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5284   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5285   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5286   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5287     return false;
5288   }
5289 
5290   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5291   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5292   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5293   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5294 
5295   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5296   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5297   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5298   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5299   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5300   set_result(enc);
5301   clear_upper_avx();
5302 
5303   return true;
5304 }
5305 
5306 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5307 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5308   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5309 
5310   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5311   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5312     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5313   }
5314   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5315 
5316   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5317 
5318   // no receiver because it is a static method
5319   Node* x    = argument(0);
5320   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5321   Node* y    = argument(2);
5322   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5323   Node* z    = argument(4);
5324 
5325   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5326   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5327 
5328   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5329   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5330   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5331   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5332   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5333       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5334     // failed array check
5335     return false;
5336   }
5337 
5338   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5339   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5340   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5341     return false;
5342   }
5343 
5344   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5345   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5346   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5347   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5348     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5349 
5350     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5351     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5352     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5353     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5354 
5355     // Allocate the result array
5356     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5357     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5358     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5359 
5360     IdealKit ideal(this);
5361 
5362 #define __ ideal.
5363      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5364      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5365      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5366      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5367      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5368      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5369        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5370      } __ else_(); {
5371        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5372        sync_kit(ideal);
5373        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5374        cast->init_req(0, control());
5375        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5376        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5377 
5378        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5379        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5380        __ sync_kit(this);
5381        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5382          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5383        } __ end_if();
5384      } __ end_if();
5385 
5386      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5387        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5388        sync_kit(ideal);
5389        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5390        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5391        __ sync_kit(this);
5392        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5393      } __ end_if();
5394 
5395      sync_kit(ideal);
5396      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5397      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5398      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5399      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5400      final_sync(ideal);
5401 #undef __
5402 
5403     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5404 
5405     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5406                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5407                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5408                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5409   } // original reexecute is set back here
5410 
5411   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5412   set_result(z);
5413   return true;
5414 }
5415 
5416 //-------------inline_squareToLen------------------------------------
5417 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_squareToLen() {
5418   assert(UseSquareToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5419 
5420   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::squareToLen();
5421   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5422     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5423   }
5424   const char* stubName = "squareToLen";
5425 
5426   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "implSquareToLen has 4 parameters");
5427 
5428   Node* x    = argument(0);
5429   Node* len  = argument(1);
5430   Node* z    = argument(2);
5431   Node* zlen = argument(3);
5432 
5433   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5434   z = must_be_not_null(z, true);
5435 
5436   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5437   const Type* z_type = z->Value(&_gvn);
5438   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5439   const TypeAryPtr* top_z = z_type->isa_aryptr();
5440   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5441       top_z  == NULL || top_z->klass()  == NULL) {
5442     // failed array check
5443     return false;
5444   }
5445 
5446   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5447   BasicType z_elem = z_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5448   if (x_elem != T_INT || z_elem != T_INT) {
5449     return false;
5450   }
5451 
5452 
5453   Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5454   Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), z_elem);
5455 
5456   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5457                                   OptoRuntime::squareToLen_Type(),
5458                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5459                                   x_start, len, z_start, zlen);
5460 
5461   set_result(z);
5462   return true;
5463 }

5465 //-------------inline_mulAdd------------------------------------------
5466 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_mulAdd() {
5467   assert(UseMulAddIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5468 
5469   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::mulAdd();
5470   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5471     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5472   }
5473   const char* stubName = "mulAdd";
5474 
5475   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "mulAdd has 5 parameters");
5476 
5477   Node* out      = argument(0);
5478   Node* in       = argument(1);
5479   Node* offset   = argument(2);
5480   Node* len      = argument(3);
5481   Node* k        = argument(4);
5482 
5483   out = must_be_not_null(out, true);
5484 
5485   const Type* out_type = out->Value(&_gvn);
5486   const Type* in_type = in->Value(&_gvn);
5487   const TypeAryPtr* top_out = out_type->isa_aryptr();
5488   const TypeAryPtr* top_in = in_type->isa_aryptr();
5489   if (top_out  == NULL || top_out->klass()  == NULL ||
5490       top_in == NULL || top_in->klass() == NULL) {
5491     // failed array check
5492     return false;
5493   }
5494 
5495   BasicType out_elem = out_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5496   BasicType in_elem = in_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5497   if (out_elem != T_INT || in_elem != T_INT) {
5498     return false;
5499   }
5500 
5501   Node* outlen = load_array_length(out);
5502   Node* new_offset = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(outlen, offset));
5503   Node* out_start = array_element_address(out, intcon(0), out_elem);
5504   Node* in_start = array_element_address(in, intcon(0), in_elem);
5505 
5506   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5507                                   OptoRuntime::mulAdd_Type(),
5508                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5509                                   out_start,in_start, new_offset, len, k);
5510   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5511   set_result(result);
5512   return true;
5513 }

5518   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5519     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5520   }

5526

5528   Node* b    = argument(1);
5529   Node* n    = argument(2);
5530   Node* len  = argument(3);
5531   Node* inv  = argument(4);
5532   Node* m    = argument(6);
5533 
5534   const Type* a_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5535   const TypeAryPtr* top_a = a_type->isa_aryptr();
5536   const Type* b_type = b->Value(&_gvn);
5537   const TypeAryPtr* top_b = b_type->isa_aryptr();
5538   const Type* n_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5539   const TypeAryPtr* top_n = n_type->isa_aryptr();
5540   const Type* m_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5541   const TypeAryPtr* top_m = m_type->isa_aryptr();
5542   if (top_a  == NULL || top_a->klass()  == NULL ||
5543       top_b == NULL || top_b->klass()  == NULL ||
5544       top_n == NULL || top_n->klass()  == NULL ||
5545       top_m == NULL || top_m->klass()  == NULL) {
5546     // failed array check
5547     return false;
5548   }

5551   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5552   BasicType n_elem = n_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5553   BasicType m_elem = m_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();

5555     return false;
5556   }

5558   // Make the call
5559   {
5560     Node* a_start = array_element_address(a, intcon(0), a_elem);
5561     Node* b_start = array_element_address(b, intcon(0), b_elem);
5562     Node* n_start = array_element_address(n, intcon(0), n_elem);
5563     Node* m_start = array_element_address(m, intcon(0), m_elem);
5564 
5565     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5566                                    OptoRuntime::montgomeryMultiply_Type(),
5567                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5568                                    a_start, b_start, n_start, len, inv, top(),
5569                                    m_start);

5630 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5631   address stubAddr = NULL;
5632   const char* stubName = NULL;
5633 
5634   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5635   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5636     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5637   }
5638 
5639   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5640 
5641   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5642 
5643   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5644   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5645   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5646   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5647   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5648 
5649   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5650   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5651   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5652   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5653   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5654       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5655     return false;
5656   }
5657 
5658   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5659   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5660   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5661     return false;
5662   }
5663 
5664   // Make the call
5665   {
5666     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5667     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5668 
5669     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5670                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5671                                    stubAddr,
5672                                    stubName,
5673                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5674                                    newArr_start,
5675                                    oldArr_start,
5676                                    newIdx,
5677                                    shiftCount,
5678                                    numIter);
5679   }
5680 
5681   return true;
5682 }

5689   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5690     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5691   }

5693   int size_l = callee()->signature()->size();
