5729 /**
5730  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5731  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5732  */
5733 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5734   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5735   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5736   // no receiver since it is static method
5737   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5738   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5739 
5740   /*
5741    *    int c = ~ crc;
5742    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5743    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5744    *    crc = ~b;
5745    */
5746 
5747   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5748   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5749   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5750   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5751 
5752   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5753   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5754   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5755   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5756 
5757   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5758   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5759   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5760   set_result(result);
5761   return true;
5762 }
5763 
5764 /**
5765  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5766  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5767  */
5768 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5769   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5770   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5771   // no receiver since it is static method
5772   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5773   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5774   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5775   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5776 
5777   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5778   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5779   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5780     // failed array check
5781     return false;
5782   }
5783 
5784   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5785   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5786   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5787     return false;
5788   }
5789 
5790   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5791   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5792   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5793 
5794   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5795   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5796 
5797   // Call the stub.
5798   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5799   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5800 
5801   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5802                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5803                                  crc, src_start, length);
5804   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5805   set_result(result);
5806   return true;
5807 }

5809 /**
5810  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5811  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5812  */
5813 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5814   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5815   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5816   // no receiver since it is static method
5817   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5818   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5819   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5820   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5821 
5822   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5823   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5824   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5825 
5826   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5827   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5828 
5829   // Call the stub.
5830   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5831   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5832 
5833   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5834                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5835                                  crc, src_start, length);
5836   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5837   set_result(result);
5838   return true;
5839 }

5843   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5844   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5845 
5846   return table;

5854 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {

5858   // no receiver since it is a static method

5860   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5861   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5862   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5863

5865

5964   }
5965 
5966   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5967   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5968   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5969     return false;
5970   }
5971 
5972   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5973   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5974 
5975   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5976   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5977 
5978   // Call the stub.
5979   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
5980   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
5981 
5982   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
5983                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5984                                  crc, src_start, length);
5985   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5986   set_result(result);
5987   return true;
5988 }
5989 
5990 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
5991 //
5992 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
5993 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5994 //
5995 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
5996   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
5997   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5998   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5999   // no receiver since it is static method
6000   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6001   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6002   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6003   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6004 
6005   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6006   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6007   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6008 
6009   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6010   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6011 
6012   // Call the stub.
6013   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6014   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6015 
6016   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6017                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6018                                  crc, src_start, length);
6019 
6020   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6021   set_result(result);
6022   return true;
6023 }
6024 
6025 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6026 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6027 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6028   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset();
6029 
6030   // Get the argument:
6031   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6032   if (stopped()) return true;
6033 
6034   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6035   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6036   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6037   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6038   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6039                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6040                                                      false);
6041   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6042 
6043   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6044   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6045 
6046   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6047   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6048 
6049   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6050   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6051   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6052   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6053   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6054 
6055   set_result(result);
6056   return true;
6057 }
6058 
6059 
6060 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6061                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6062                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6063   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6064     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6065     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6066     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6067     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6068     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6069   } else {
6070     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6071   }
6072   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6073                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6074                                               is_static);
6075 
6076   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6077   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6078 
6079   if (is_static) {
6080     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6081     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6082   }
6083 
6084   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6085 
6086   // Compute address and memory type.
6087   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6088   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6089   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6090   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6091   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6092   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6093   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6094 
6095   // Build the resultant type of the load
6096   const Type *type;
6097   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6098     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6099   } else {
6100     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6101   }
6102 
6103   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6104 
6105   if (is_vol) {
6106     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6107   }
6108 
6109   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6110 }
6111 
6112 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6113                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6114                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6115   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6116     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6117     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6118     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6119     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6120     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6121   }
6122   else {
6123     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6124   }
6125   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6126     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6127     is_static);
6128 
6129   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6130   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6131 
6132   if (is_static) {
6133     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6134     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6135   }
6136 
6137   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6138 
6139   // Compute address and memory type.
6140   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6141   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6142 
6143   return adr;
6144 }

6146 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6147 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6148   address stubAddr = NULL;
6149   const char *stubName;
6150   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6151 
6152   switch(id) {
6153   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6154     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6155     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6156     break;
6157   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6158     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6159     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6160     break;
6161   default:
6162     break;
6163   }
6164   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6165 
6166   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6167   Node* src             = argument(1);
6168   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6169   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6170   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6171 
6172   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6173   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6174 
6175   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6176   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6177   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6178   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6179   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6180   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6181 
6182   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6183   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6184   Node* src_start  = src;
6185   Node* dest_start = dest;
6186   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6187     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6188     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6189     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6190   }
6191 
6192   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6193   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6194   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6195   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6196 
6197   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6198     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6199     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6200     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6201     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6202 
6203     // Call the stub.
6204     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6205                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6206                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6207   } else {
6208     // Call the stub.
6209     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6210                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6211                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6212   }
6213 
6214   return true;
6215 }
6216 
6217 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6218 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6219   address stubAddr = NULL;
6220   const char *stubName = NULL;
6221 
6222   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6223 
6224   switch(id) {
6225   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6226     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6227     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6228     break;
6229   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6230     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6231     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6232     break;
6233   default:
6234     break;
6235   }
6236   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6237 
6238   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6239   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6240   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6241   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6242   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6243   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6244 
6245   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6246   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6247 
6248   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6249   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6250   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6251   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6252   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6253   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6254           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6255 
6256   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6257   Node* src_start  = src;
6258   Node* dest_start = dest;
6259   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6260     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6261     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6262     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6263   }
6264 
6265   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6266   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6267   // so we cast it here safely.
6268   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6269 
6270   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6271   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6272 
6273   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6274   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6275   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6276   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6277   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6278   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6279 
6280   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6281   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6282   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6283   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6284   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6285 
6286   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6287   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6288   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6289 
6290   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6291   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6292   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6293   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6294 
6295   Node* cbcCrypt;
6296   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6297     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6298     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6299     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6300     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6301 
6302     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6303     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6304                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6305                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6306                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6307   } else {
6308     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6309     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6310                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6311                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6312                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6313   }
6314 
6315   // return cipher length (int)
6316   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6317   set_result(retvalue);
6318   return true;
6319 }

6458   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6459   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6460   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6461   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6462   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6463   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6464   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6465   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6466   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6467   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6468   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6469   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6470 
6471   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6472   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6473   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6474   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6475 
6476   Node* ctrCrypt;
6477   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6478     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6479     return false;
6480   }
6481   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6482   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6483                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6484                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6485                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6486 
6487   // return cipher length (int)
6488   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6489   set_result(retvalue);
6490   return true;
6491 }
6492 
6493 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6494 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6495 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6496   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6497   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6498   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6499   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6500   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6501   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6502   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6503     return (Node *) NULL;
6504   }
6505   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6506 #else
6507   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6508 #endif // PPC64
6509   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6510   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6511 
6512   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6513   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6514   return k_start;
6515 }
6516 
6517 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6518 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6519   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6520   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6521   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6522 
6523   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6524   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6525   return original_k_start;
6526 }
6527 
6528 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6529 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6530 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6531 // for encryption:
6532 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6533 // for decryption:
6534 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6535 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6536 //
6537 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6538   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6539   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6540 
6541   Node* src = argument(1);
6542   Node* dest = argument(4);
6543 
6544   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6545   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6546 
6547   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6548   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6549   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6550   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6551   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6552   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6553 
6554   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6555   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6556   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6557     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6558     Node* ctrl = control();
6559     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6560     return ctrl;
6561   }
6562 
6563   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6564   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6565 
6566   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6567   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6568 
6569   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6570   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6571   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6572 
6573   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6574 
6575   // for encryption, we are done
6576   if (!decrypting)
6577     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6578 
6579   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6580   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6581   // see the original java code for why.
6582   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6583   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6584 
6585   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6586   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6587   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6588   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6589 
6590   record_for_igvn(region);
6591   return _gvn.transform(region);
6592 }
6593 
6594 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6595 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6596 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6597 // for encryption:
6598 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6599 // for decryption:
6600 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6601 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6602 //
6603 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6604   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6605   Node* objECB = argument(0);
6606 
6607   // Load embeddedCipher field of ElectronicCodeBook object.
6608   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6609 
6610   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6611   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6612   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object
6613   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objECB)->isa_instptr();
6614   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6615   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6616 
6617   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6618   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6619   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6620     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6621     Node* ctrl = control();
6622     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6623     return ctrl;
6624   }
6625   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6626 
6627   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6628   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6629   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6630 
6631   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6632 
6633   // for encryption, we are done
6634   if (!decrypting)
6635     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6636 
6637   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6638   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6639   // see the original java code for why.
6640   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6641   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6642   Node* src = argument(1);
6643   Node* dest = argument(4);
6644   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6645   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6646   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6647   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6648 
6649   record_for_igvn(region);
6650   return _gvn.transform(region);
6651 }

6695 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6696 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {
6697   address stubAddr;
6698   const char *stubName;
6699   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6700 
6701   stubAddr = StubRoutines::ghash_processBlocks();
6702   stubName = "ghash_processBlocks";
6703 
6704   Node* data           = argument(0);
6705   Node* offset         = argument(1);
6706   Node* len            = argument(2);
6707   Node* state          = argument(3);
6708   Node* subkeyH        = argument(4);
6709 
6710   state = must_be_not_null(state, true);
6711   subkeyH = must_be_not_null(subkeyH, true);
6712   data = must_be_not_null(data, true);
6713 
6714   Node* state_start  = array_element_address(state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6715   assert(state_start, "state is NULL");
6716   Node* subkeyH_start  = array_element_address(subkeyH, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6717   assert(subkeyH_start, "subkeyH is NULL");
6718   Node* data_start  = array_element_address(data, offset, T_BYTE);
6719   assert(data_start, "data is NULL");
6720 
6721   Node* ghash = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6722                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
6723                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6724                                   state_start, subkeyH_start, data_start, len);
6725   return true;
6726 }

6760 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6761 //
6762 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6763 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6764 //
6765 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6766 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6767 //
6768 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6769 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6770 //
6771 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6772   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6773 
6774   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6775   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6776   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6777 
6778   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6779   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6780   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6781     // failed array check
6782     return false;
6783   }
6784   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6785   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6786   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6787     return false;
6788   }
6789   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6790   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6791   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6792   Node* state = NULL;
6793   address stubAddr;
6794   const char *stubName;
6795 
6796   switch(id) {
6797   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6798     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6799     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6800     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6801     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6802     break;
6803   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6804     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6805     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6806     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6807     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6808     break;
6809   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6810     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6811     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6812     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6813     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6814     break;
6815   default:
6816     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6817     return false;
6818   }
6819   if (state == NULL) return false;
6820 
6821   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6822   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6823 
6824   // Call the stub.
6825   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6826                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6827                                  src_start, state);
6828 
6829   return true;
6830 }
6831 
6832 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6833 //
6834 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6835 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6836 //
6837 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6838   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6839          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6840   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6841   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6842 
6843   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6844   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6845   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6846   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6847 
6848   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6849   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6850   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6851     // failed array check
6852     return false;
6853   }
6854   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6855   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6856   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6857     return false;
6858   }
6859   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6860   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6861   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6862 
6863   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6864   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6865   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6866   bool        long_state = false;
6867 
6868   switch (predicate) {
6869   case 0:
6870     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress)) {
6871       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6872       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6873       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6874     }
6875     break;
6876   case 1:
6877     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress)) {
6878       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6879       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6880       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6881     }
6882     break;
6883   case 2:
6884     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress)) {
6885       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6886       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6887       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6888       long_state = true;
6889     }
6890     break;
6891   default:
6892     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6893   }
6894   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6895     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6896     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6897 
6898     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6899     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6900     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6901     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6902 
6903     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6904     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6905     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6906     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6907   }
6908   return false;
6909 }
6910 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6911 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6912                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6913                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6914   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6915   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6916   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6917   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6918 
6919   Node* state;
6920   if (long_state) {
6921     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6922   } else {
6923     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6924   }
6925   if (state == NULL) return false;
6926 
6927   // Call the stub.
6928   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6929                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6930                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6931                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6932   // return ofs (int)
6933   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6934   set_result(result);
6935 
6936   return true;
6937 }
6938 
6939 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6940 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6941   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6942   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6943   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6944 
6945   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6946   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6947   return state;
6948 }
6949 
6950 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6951 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6952   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6953   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6954   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6955 
6956   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6957   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6958   return state;
6959 }
6960 
6961 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6962 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6963 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6964 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6965 //
6966 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6967   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6968          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6969   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6970 
6971   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6972   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
6973 
6974   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
6975   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
6976   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
6977   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6978 
6979   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6980   switch (predicate) {
6981   case 0:
6982     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6983       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
6984       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6985     }
6986     break;
6987   case 1:
6988     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6989       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
6990       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6991     }
6992     break;
6993   case 2:
6994     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6995       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
6996       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6997     }
6998     break;
6999   default:
7000     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7001   }
7002 
7003   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7004   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7005     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7006   }
7007   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7008     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7009     Node* ctrl = control();
7010     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7011     return ctrl;
7012   }
7013   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7014 
7015   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7016   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7017   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7018   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7019 
7020   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7021 }
7022 
7023 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7024 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7025   Node *a = NULL;
7026   Node *b = NULL;
7027   Node *c = NULL;
7028   Node* result = NULL;
7029   switch (id) {
7030   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7031     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7032     // no receiver since it is static method
7033     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7034     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7035     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7036     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7037     break;
7038   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7039     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7040     a = argument(0);
7041     b = argument(1);
7042     c = argument(2);
7043     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7044     break;
7045   default:
7046     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7047   }
7048   set_result(result);
7049   return true;
7050 }
7051 
7052 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7053   // argument(0) is receiver
7054   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7055   Node* n = NULL;
7056 
7057   switch (id) {
7058     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7059       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7060       break;
7061     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7062       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7063       break;
7064     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7065       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7066       break;
7067     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7068       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7069       break;
7070     default:
7071       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7072   }
7073 
7074   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7075   return true;
7076 }
7077 
7078 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7079 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7080 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7081 
7082   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7083   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7084   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7085 
7086   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7087 
7088   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7089     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7090 
7091     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7092       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7093       return false;
7094     }
7095 
7096     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7097 
7098     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7099       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7100         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7101         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7102       }
7103     }
7104 
7105     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7106     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7107     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7108       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7109       return false;
7110     }
7111   }
7112 */
7113 
7114   Node *a = NULL;
7115   Node *b = NULL;
7116   Node *n = NULL;
7117   switch (id) {
7118   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7119   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7120     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7121     a = argument(0);
7122     b = argument(1);
7123     break;
7124   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7125   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7126     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7127     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7128     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7129     break;
7130   default:
7131     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7132     break;
7133   }
7134   switch (id) {
7135   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7136   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7137   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7138   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7139   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7140   }
7141   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7142   return true;
7143 }
7144 
7145 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7146   Node* counts = argument(1);
7147   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7148   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7149   if (counts->is_Con()
7150       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7151       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7152       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7153     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7154     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7155     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7156 
7157     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7158       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7159                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7160     }
7161 
7162     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7163       // According to profile, never executed.
7164       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7165                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7166       return true;
7167     }
7168 
7169     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7170     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7171     Node* result = argument(0);
7172     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7173       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7174       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7175 
7176       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7177       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7178 
7179       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7180       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7181       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7182 
7183       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7184         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7185         // the value has been seen at least once.
7186         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7187         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7188         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7189 
7190         set_control(slow_path);
7191         set_i_o(i_o());
7192 
7193         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7194                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7195       }
7196       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7197       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7198       // later on.
7199       set_control(fast_path);
7200       result = intcon(expected_val);
7201     }
7202     // Stop profiling.
7203     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7204     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7205     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7206     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7207     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7208     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7209     set_result(profile);
7210     return true;
7211   } else {
7212     // Continue profiling.
7213     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7214     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7215     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7216     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7217     return false;
7218   }
7219 }
7220 
7221 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7222   Node* n = argument(0);
7223   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7224   return true;
7225 }
